< review>
My family decided to give this place a try because of the high reviews.....It was dreadful. Our first pizza was burned, black edges and very dark brown crust.
When we called they said they would make us another one. When I picked up the new pizza the were completely unapologetic and condescending, opening it in my face and asking "is this one okay?" ( If you dont know the answer to that question and thought the first was good, then you shouldn't be making Pizza)
Sadly the (good) pizza wasnt good either. The crust was still overdone, dry, and tasted kind of burned. There was too much cheese distributed unevenly and caked together, but the worst part was the sauce.
I love spicy food, but you shouldnt make your base sauce too spicy that kids cant eat it, if somebody wants spicy pizza they can add red pepper.
Like some other reviews mentioned, the sauce was way too spicy for my child to eat. So after all the money spent, two trips, I still didnt have edible food for my family. TRASH, not going back.</review>

<review>First- Shout Outs to some incredible instructors who are NOT there to fail you or to demean you. Sam- Class Instructor was PHENOMENAL! She constantly responded to emails, she is able to take the most complicated concept and break it down for you to understand it. I requested a lot of clarifications and was able to study with here one on one on an off day. Her commitment to a student who puts 100% in is unparalleled.

Shout outs to the skills instructors Dan(This old salt who had a really big heart and YEARS of knowledge) RJ and Sarah (both Compassionate and Dedicated to ensuring you understand, def mood lifters). While I should take the time to state that the program could be improved if a Guide on the Skills was given to each student instead of each student writing it down themselves- this would ensure continuity across the Skills Instructors; it should be noted the Skills Instructors we‚Äôre aware of these issues and were more worried about the student understanding the major concepts to be prepared for the real world and NREMT exam/test. (Example: One instructor stated to wrap the thumbs togeather whereas another instructor told us not too)

The FULLTIME program itself: a ROUGH INTENSE 5 weeks. Its actuality 4 weeks of class with the 5th week consisting of tests. (150 Multiple Choice Final and a Skills Practical) Class started at 0800 M,T,W, TH. It ended around 1600 everyday (some days going to 1700) with an hour for lunch. They do NOT go over every chapter in the Orange book. You are expected to read Chapters by yourself. By biggest recommendation is to Read Chapter 1-6 (or more!) before taking the course. I had to email Matt as this information was NOT put out ahead of time. I would recommend to read and annotate in the book as opposed to taking notes as you will be taking notes in class about the chapters.

Note that Wednesday‚Äôs are Skills days and are half day. Groups of 6-8 will learn skills togeather.

All of your paperwork isn‚Äôt due until the end of the last week, but get it all done before class starts. The three days you have ‚Äúoff‚Äù are chockerblocked with filling out Study Guides, Sign and Symptoms Notebook, and Reading the Book. (Each chapter takes about 1-2 hours to read).

Do not expect to have any down time or time off. I didn‚Äôt do anything but this course for the entire 5 weeks. It was mentally exhausting. (I had a cheat afternoon every week on Friday or Saturday where I would hang with friends)

We started with 40 and ended with 32 because many students didn‚Äôt realize the time commitment or intensity of the course. In addition, the tests are pretty hard. The Midterm and Final pull from the Orange Book- but it can be anything that has been discussed. Studying is a MUST. I‚Äôd recommend putting the S/S in a Xcel file btw!

Last but not least: the Facilities are lacking any type of water machine and for the 5 weeks I was there, the refrigerator at the Anahaiem campus has black mold in it and the vending machines did not work properly. Being a water bottle! The bathrooms and classroom are wicked nice though! There is a bunch of teaching aids that are in good condition as well :)

Overall: I am very happy with my investment with time and money. I can‚Äôt thank the instructors enough! But the program could be Improved through standardized Skills Guides for the student, a Water Machine for the Campus, and alerting students to read at least two weeks in advance for the course.<//review><user>106193513957592514008</user></record>

<Review>this is just a reflection of my personal experience here. i was in the weekend course classes for their 12 week program. you take 4 test and 4 quizzes and you have to get an average of 80% in order to get the opportunity to take the final exam. This final is pass/no pass, so even if you had a 99% average but fail the final you fail the ENTIRE class. If you pass the final then you have the opportunity to take the NREMT.

For my class ~60 people started ~25 achieved the 80% or higher average, and ~only 10 passed the class :/ that‚Äôs only 6%!!!

The class is $1000 + ~$100 for uniform and ~$100 for the homework code/book.

this class will teach you a lot and prepare you for the field if you take everything away with you regardless if you pass or fail.< /Review>< Name>

Just finished my 5 week Full Time Course at WCEMT and believe me its full time. This class will take all of your time for 5 weeks. WCEMT is well known and will help you get hired fast.

My personal experience I came in with absolutely zero medical experience and after these 5 weeks I feel ready and qualified to get in an ambulance and start running calls.  I feel confident in my knowledge and want to continue learning more. I recommend reading your text book before class and getting a good understanding of the Airway Breathing and Circulation of blood through the body before class starts, it will help later. Ulta Beauty is a great "one stop shop" store. You can get a variety of products there and even services such as hair coloring, haircuts, makeup applications/classes, eye brow arching/eyelashes. They carry the top brands in haircare, skincare, makeup, fragrances and all things "beauty". The prices are not nominal, but they have a great return policy, so if you try a product and don't love it, you have sixty days to return for a full refund (just save your receipts).< /Review>

<Time>1512784864205</Time><rate>5< /rate>< review>
I hadn't been to see a dentist in 17 years.   I dont have a particular reason- just never had any pain.  But with that said, All people that are afraid of the dentist should have gone with me today.  I had 2 appointments today.  From the moment I walked in I was helped by some very beautiful young ladies and seated. I was called to meet the ortho and a young- also beautiful woman began to prep me and answered any and all questions I had.   I met the ortho surgeon who was male and also very nice. ( My teeth are drifting apart and I was concerned I would have rotten teeth, unusable for braces  It had been 17 years afterall.)  I was given a good examination by somebody with knowledge. I was deemed good for braces.  I have no money so it's for the future.
My 2nd appt was for a cleaning- I really feared bad news from the dentist.  I was called 10 min after my prior appt. I had x rays done and had to bite on plastic which wasn't so bad I just have a small gag reflex with the plastic throwaway sleeve they cover the biting part with.  The gorgeous young lady that took the xrays was also extremely helpful in any of the Q&A I had.  I was moved to a different room where they would actually do the cleaning.  I met the dentist-  This guy was middle aged and cracking jokes.  He is awesome.  I feared his news after a young woman(also beautiful) came and took different pictures of my teeth and.. dried them.  The dentist saw me and had me open wide, he searched for cavities and other complications and found none- which is awesome! Yay Me!  After sooo long of not seeing a dentist I really didnt expect that.  I try to take care of my teeth but I dont floss.  It was now time for my cleaning.  I think I am like everyone when I say having power tools in your mouth can be quite scary.  But, BUT- they've made leaps and bounds in dentistry since 17 years ago.  The tools are very small and not very noisy.  I braced for some sort of pain while they turned on the tool and started cleaning- there was none.  The most awkward anything was the sensation of the tool doing its job in front and behind my teeth.  My dentist finished cleaning , cracked some more jokes and ran off to some other beautiful smile to help.  A young woman chatted with me while finishing with flouride and asked me to rate them and so I am here!  These guys kick ass, All of em! Everyone that I spoke to or had questions with was genuinely professional,  pleasant, and courteous. ... and beautiful.

I understand that wait times could be different and that you may need more than just a cleaning.  In my experience when you find a good place filled with heartfelt, wonderful people,- it normally stays that way.  This Western Dental has it in spades and I recommend any and all to go and check em out.

Sorry to all at Western Dental in Banning I am extremely horrible with names.  You guys keep kickin ass, I'll see you guys soon :)</review>
